<script type='text/javascript'>//<![CDATA[
window.addEvent('load', function() {
/**
* requestAnimationFrame shim
*/
var lastTime = 0
, vendors = ['ms', 'moz', 'webkit', 'o'];

for (var x = 0; x < vendors.length && !window.requestAnimationFrame; ++x) {
window.requestAnimationFrame = window[vendors[x]+'RequestAnimationFrame'];
window.cancelAnimationFrame = window[vendors[x]+'CancelAnimationFrame'] || window[vendors[x]+'CancelRequestAnimationFrame'];
}

if (!window.requestAnimationFrame)
window.requestAnimationFrame = function(callback, element) {
var currTime = new Date().getTime();
var timeToCall = Math.max(0, 16 - (currTime - lastTime));
var id = window.setTimeout(function() { callback(currTime + timeToCall); },
timeToCall);
lastTime = currTime + timeToCall;
return id;
};

if (!window.cancelAnimationFrame)
window.cancelAnimationFrame = function(id) {
clearTimeout(id);
};


/**
* Init
*/
var canvas1 = document.getElementById('c1')
, canvas2 = document.getElementById('c2')
, canvas3 = document.getElementById('c2')
, ctx = canvas1.getContext("2d")
, ctx2 = canvas2.getContext("2d")
, ctx3 = canvas3.getContext("2d")
, sourceImage = new Image()
, nextImage = new Image()
;

UjbKo/sfdj/p6/wDsK87oprD0k7pC9tPuent8Xg3XQu2P+Pv/AOwpg+La7wx0LOO32v8A+wrzOirjTjF3SE5yfU9TT4xhBgaAMZz/AMff/wBro/4XL1A0HA9Ptn/2FeWUV0+3qdzOx6iPjEQTjQuvXN3n/wBkpD8YTnP9h/8Ak3/9hXl9FNYmquouVHp//C3xnP8AYZ9/9M6/+OUH4vLu3DQBn/r7/wDsK8wop/Wq38wciPTz8XwTn+wsY/6e/wD7Cmt8XicY0TGP+nv/AOwrzKij63W/mDkiemP8XGcf8gQD/t6/+wpD8W9y4bRD+F3j/wBkrzSij63W/mFyR7H/2Q==");


/**
* Start effect
*/
sourceImage.onload = function() {
var width = canvas2.width
, height = canvas2.height
, sourceData, newImage, distortedImage
, seed = 0
, reverse = false
;

ctx.drawImage(sourceImage, 0, 0);
ctx2.createImageData(width, height);
ctx3.drawImage(nextImage, 0, 0);
sourceData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
newImage = ctx2.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);
nextImage = ctx3.getImageData(0, 0, width, height);

function distort() {
distortedImage = waveDistortion(sourceData, newImage, reverse ? seed-=4 : seed+=4, {
'freq': 1 + Math.random() * 10
, 'amplitude': 5
, 'tear': 10 + Math.random() * 10
, 'noise': true
, 'noiseMiltiplier': 5
}
);
ctx2.putImageData(distortedImage, 0, 0);

if (seed > height/16) {
sourceData = nextImage;
reverse = true;
}

if (seed == 0) {
ctx2.putImageData(sourceData, 0, 0);
return false;
}

return true;
}

function animate() {
var aId = requestAnimationFrame( animate );
var result = distort();
if (!result) {
cancelAnimationFrame(aId);
};
}

animate();
};


/**
* Distortion effect
*
* @param {ImageData} sourceImage Original image
* @param {ImageData} newImage Destination image (may be filled with transparent black)
* @param {Number} seed Effect origin offset
* @param {Object} opts Effect options
*/
function waveDistortion(sourceImage, newImage, seed, opts) {
var offset = []
, newImageData = newImage.data
, sourceImageData = sourceImage.data
, width = sourceImage.width
, height = sourceImage.height
, i, o, x, y
, sourceIndex, destIndex, start
, noiseValue = 0
, freq, tear
;

opts = opts || {}
opts.freq = opts.freq || 2;
opts.amplitude = opts.amplitude || 1
opts.tear = opts.tear || 2;
opts.noise = opts.noise || false;
opts.noiseMiltiplier = opts.noiseMiltiplier || 2.2

for (o = 0; o < height; ++o) {
offset[o] = [];
for (i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
// sin() controls frequency, tan() controls speed and quantity of tears
freq = Math.sin( o/((seed + i) * (1/opts.freq)) ) * opts.amplitude;
tear = Math.tan( (Math.pow(seed, opts.tear) + o)/height );
offset[o][i] = ((0.5 + (0.5 + freq * tear) << 0) * 4) << 0; // fast rounding, otherwise webkit craps out
}
}

// distortion loop
for (x = 0; x < height; ++x) {
for (y = 0; y < width; ++y) {
sourceIndex = destIndex = start = (x * width + y) * 4
;

// apply noise
if (opts.noise) {
//noiseValue = Math.pow(seed, opts.noiseMiltiplier) * (Math.random() - 0.5);
noiseValue = Math.exp(seed/opts.noiseMiltiplier) * (Math.random() - 0.5);
}

// copy pixels to target image
for (i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
destIndex = start + offset[x][i];

newImageData[destIndex + i] = sourceImageData[sourceIndex + i] + noiseValue;
newImageData[destIndex + 3] = sourceImageData[sourceIndex + 3];
}
}
}

return newImage;
}



});//]]>

</script>
